### 14.5 重点能力详细定义示例

以下以`collect.t2i.sft.crawl`(文生图SFT爬虫采集)为例，展示完整的Capability定义：

```python
# capabilities_v2/definitions/collect_t2i_sft_crawl.py
capability_definition = {
    "id": "collect.t2i.sft.crawl",
    "name": "文生图SFT爬虫采集",
    "category": "collect",
    "model_type": "text_to_image",
    "phase": "sft",
    "path": "crawl",  # 纯采集，非合成
    "description": "通过Web爬虫从公开数据源采集图像-描述对，用于文生图模型的SFT训练。",
    
    "input_schema": {
        "type": "object",
        "properties": {
            "seed_urls": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "target_count": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 1000, "maximum": 10000000},
            "filters": {
                "min_resolution": {"type": "integer", "default": 256},
                "min_description_length": {"type": "integer", "default": 10},
                "language": {"type": "string", "enum": ["en", "zh", "all"], "default": "en"},
                "exclude_nsfw": {"type": "boolean", "default": True},
                "exclude_watermark": {"type": "boolean", "default": True}
            },
            "output_format": {"type": "string", "enum": ["webdataset", "jsonl"], "default": "webdataset"}
        },
        "required": ["seed_urls", "target_count"]
    },
    
    "processing_pipeline": [
        {"step": 1, "name": "url_resolve", "desc": "解析种子URL，生成采集队列"},
        {"step": 2, "name": "parallel_fetch", "desc": "Playwright并发抓取"},
        {"step": 3, "name": "image_extract", "desc": "提取图像及ALT文本"},
        {"step": 4, "name": "filter_apply", "desc": "应用分辨率/长度/语言/NSFW/水印过滤"},
        {"step": 5, "name": "format_convert", "desc": "统一格式与存储"},
        {"step": 6, "name": "metadata_gen", "desc": "生成元数据JSONL"}
    ],
    
    "dependencies": ["clean.image.basic", "clean.image.nsfw", "clean.image.watermark"]
}
```


### 14.6 能力调用实现

```python
# capabilities_v2/engine.py
class CapabilityRegistry:
    def __init__(self):
        self._capabilities = {}
        self._load_all_definitions()  # 加载217个能力定义
    
    async def invoke(self, cap_id: str, inputs: Dict, actor: str = None, 
                     refs: Dict = None) -> CapabilityResult:
        cap = self._capabilities.get(cap_id)
        if not cap:
            raise CapabilityNotFoundError(cap_id)
        
        # 根据能力类型路由到对应执行器
        if cap.category.startswith("collect"):
            # 采集层 — 只执行真实数据采集，绝不合成
            result = await self._execute_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("synth"):
            # 合成层 — 只执行AI模型合成生成
            result = await self._execute_synth(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("clean"):
            result = await self._execute_clean(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("dedupe"):
            result = await self._execute_dedupe(cap, inputs, refs)
        # ... 其他层级
        
        # 审计、血缘、指标记录
        await self._post_process(cap, inputs, result, actor)
        
        return CapabilityResult(status="success", outputs=result)
```

### 14.7 能力分类体系升级说明 (V5.0 → V5.1)

本次能力设计进行了**全面重构**，核心变更如下：

#### 变更1: 从混合分类 → 按数据生产全链路分层

| 维度 | V5.0 (旧) | V5.1 (新) |
|---|---|---|
| 分类依据 | 业务域 (project/dataset/agent) | **数据生产全链路层级** (采集→清洗→去重→合成→标注→质检→导出→版本→血缘) |
| 能力数量 | 140+ | **217** |
| 采集层 | 15个 (混在crawler中) | **83个** (按模型类型+训练阶段细分) |
| 合成层 | 不存在 | **34个** (新增) |

#### 变更2: 新增"合成层" (Synthesis Layer)

合成层是通过AI模型(扩散模型/LLM/视频模型/3D模型/TTS)生成全新训练数据，与采集层并列构成**数据生产双通道**:

```
通道一: 采集通道 (83个能力)  →  真实数据采集
通道二: 合成通道 (34个能力)  →  AI模型合成生成
```

#### 变更3: 采集层按模型类型+训练阶段细分

| 模型类型 | Pre-train | SFT | DPO | RL | LoRA | 合计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Text-to-Image | 2 | 3 | 2 | 1 | 2 | 10 |
| Image-to-Image | 0 | 1 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 3 |
| Image Editing | 0 | 2 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 4 |
| Multi-Image Edit | 0 | 2 | 0 | 0 | 0 | 2 |
| Text-to-Video | 2 | 3 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 8 |
| Image-to-Video | 0 | 1 | 1 | 0 | 0 | 2 |
| Multi-I2V | 0 | 2 | 0 | 0 | 0 | 2 |
| Text-to-3D | 2 | 1 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 5 |
| Image-to-3D | 0 | 1 | 0 | 0 | 0 | 1 |
| Multi-I2D | 0 | 2 | 0 | 0 | 0 | 2 |
| Audio/TTS/ASR | 2 | 3 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 7 |
| Text/LLM | 2 | 4 | 2 | 2 | 2 | 12 |
| Agent | 0 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 4 |
| Multimodal | 2 | 2 | 1 | 0 | 0 | 5 |
| **合计** | **12** | **28** | **12** | **5** | **10** | **67** |

#### 变更4: 能力ID命名规范更新

```
新命名规范: {category}.{model_type}.{phase}.{path}

示例:
- collect.t2i.sft.crawl      → 采集层·文生图·SFT·爬虫采集
- collect.t2v.pretrain.import → 采集层·文生视频·预训练·数据集导入
- synth.t2i.sft              → 合成层·文生图·SFT·合成生成
- synth.t2v.sft              → 合成层·文生视频·SFT·合成生成
- clean.image.basic          → 清洗层·图像·基础清洗
- label.auto.image_cap       → 标注层·自动·图像描述
- export.sft.chatml          → 导出层·SFT·ChatML格式
```

#### 变更5: 数据生产双通道架构图

见14.4节完整架构图。

## 第15章 引擎层设计 (16引擎)

### 15.1 16引擎全览

| 引擎 | 文件 | 行数 | 核心职责 |
|---|---|---|---|
| ProjectEngine | `engines/project_engine.py` | ~900 | 项目生命周期管理 |
| RequirementEngine | `engines/requirement_engine.py` | ~1300 | 需求与任务管理 |
| DatasetManager | `engines/dataset_manager.py` | ~1200 | 数据集与版本管理 |
| PackEngine | `engines/pack_engine.py` | ~800 | 数据包7态状态机 |
| WorkbenchEngine | `engines/workbench_engine.py` | ~1000 | 标注与审核工作台 |
| InternalQCEngine | `engines/internal_qc_engine.py` | ~1100 | 4模式质量检测 |
| RequesterAcceptanceEngine | `engines/requester_acceptance.py` | ~500 | 需求方验收3决定 |
| DeliveryWorkflow | `engines/delivery_workflow.py` | ~600 | 交付7态状态机 |
| TransferEngine | `engines/transfer_engine.py` | ~600 | HMAC签名分享 |
| **CrawlerEngine** | `engines/crawler_engine.py` | ~1500 | 智能采集调度 |
| **AgentEngine** | `engines/agent_engine.py` | ~1800 | Agent对话与任务 |
| **OctoEngine** | `engines/octo_engine.py` | ~1400 | Agent协作网络 |
| **VidaEngine** | `engines/vida_engine.py` | ~1200 | 屏幕感知与主动行动 |
| **MetaKimEngine** | `engines/meta_kim_engine.py` | ~1400 | AI治理层 |
| **DramaEngine** | `engines/drama_engine.py` | ~1400 | AI短剧全流程 |
| **ComfyEngine** | `engines/comfy_engine.py` | ~1000 | ComfyUI工作流 |

### 15.2 DatasetManager — 数据生产全链路引擎 (完整实现)

```python
# engines/dataset_manager.py
class DatasetManager:
    """
    数据集管理引擎 — 数据生产全链路核心
    覆盖: 创建 → 采集 → 导入 → 清洗 → 标注 → 质检 → 导出 → 版本管理
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.db = SessionLocal()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
        self.cleaning_engine = CleaningEngine()
        self.dedupe_engine = DedupeEngine()
        self.label_engine = AutoLabelEngine()
        self.scoring_engine = ScoringEngine()
        self.qc_engine = InternalQCEngine()
        self.export_engine = ExportEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    # ============ 1. 创建数据集 ============
    async def create_dataset(self, name: str, modality: str, 
                             project_id: str = None, 
                             config: Dict = None) -> Dataset:
        """创建新数据集"""
        dataset = Dataset(
            id=f"ds_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=name,
            modality=modality,
            status="draft",
            project_id=project_id,
            export_config=config or {},
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(dataset)
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.created",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset.id,
            payload={"name": name, "modality": modality}
        )
        
        return dataset
    
    # ============ 2. 导入数据 (多种来源) ============
    async def import_data(self, dataset_id: str, source_type: str, 
                          source_config: Dict) -> ImportResult:
        """
        导入数据到数据集
        支持: 本地文件/OSS/S3/URL/采集任务
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        dataset.status = "importing"
        self.db.commit()
        
        imported_assets = []
        
        if source_type == "local":
            # 本地文件上传
            files = source_config.get("files", [])
            for file_path in files:
                asset = await self._import_local_file(file_path, dataset_id)
                imported_assets.append(asset)
                
        elif source_type == "oss":
            # OSS/S3导入
            bucket = source_config.get("bucket")
            prefix = source_config.get("prefix")
            assets = await self._import_from_oss(bucket, prefix, dataset_id)
            imported_assets.extend(assets)
            
        elif source_type == "crawler":
            # 从采集任务导入
            job_id = source_config.get("job_id")
            assets = await self._import_from_crawler(job_id, dataset_id)
            imported_assets.extend(assets)
            
        elif source_type == "url":
            # URL列表导入
            urls = source_config.get("urls", [])
            for url in urls:
                asset = await self._import_from_url(url, dataset_id)
                imported_assets.append(asset)
        
        # 更新统计
        dataset.total_samples = len(imported_assets)
        dataset.files_count = len(imported_assets)
        dataset.status = "processing"
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.imported",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset_id,
            payload={"source_type": source_type, "count": len(imported_assets)}
        )
        
        return ImportResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, imported_count=len(imported_assets), 
                           assets=imported_assets)
    
    async def _import_local_file(self, file_path: str, dataset_id: str) -> Asset:
        """导入本地文件"""
        file_type = self._detect_file_type(file_path)
        file_hash = self._compute_hash(file_path)
        
        # 去重检查
        existing = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.file_hash == file_hash,
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id
        ).first()
        if existing:
            return existing
        
        asset = Asset(
            id=f"asset_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
            name=os.path.basename(file_path),
            file_type=file_type,
            file_format=os.path.splitext(file_path)[1][1:],
            file_size=os.path.getsize(file_path),
            file_hash=file_hash,
            file_path=file_path,
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            status="uploaded",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        # 提取媒体信息
        if file_type == "image":
            from PIL import Image
            img = Image.open(file_path)
            asset.width = img.width
            asset.height = img.height
            asset.metadata["mode"] = img.mode
            
        elif file_type == "video":
            import cv2
            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(file_path)
            asset.width = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_WIDTH))
            asset.height = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_HEIGHT))
            asset.duration = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_COUNT) / cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)
            asset.frames = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_COUNT))
            cap.release()
            
        elif file_type == "audio":
            from pydub import AudioSegment
            audio = AudioSegment.from_file(file_path)
            asset.duration = len(audio) / 1000.0
            asset.channels = audio.channels
            asset.sample_rate = audio.frame_rate
            
        self.db.add(asset)
        self.db.commit()
        return asset
    
    # ============ 3. 数据清洗 ============
    async def clean_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, rules: Dict = None) -> CleanResult:
        """
        清洗数据集 — 8模态清洗
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status != "deleted"
        ).all()
        
        cleaned_assets = []
        rejected_assets = []
        
        for asset in assets:
            result = await self.cleaning_engine.clean(asset, rules or {})
            if result.rejected:
                rejected_assets.append(asset)
                asset.status = "rejected"
            else:
                cleaned_assets.append(asset)
                asset.status = "processed"
                # 更新清洗后的元数据
                asset.metadata.update(result.metadata)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        return CleanResult(
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            total=len(assets),
            cleaned=len(cleaned_assets),
            rejected=len(rejected_assets),
            rejected_assets=rejected_assets
        )
    
    # ============ 4. 自动打标 ============
    async def auto_label(self, dataset_id: str, schema: Dict) -> LabelResult:
        """
        自动打标 — 4策略
        """
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status == "processed"
        ).all()
        
        labeled = []
        for asset in assets:
            labels = await self.label_engine.label(asset, schema)
            asset.labels = labels
            labeled.append(asset)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 更新标签分布
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        dataset.label_distribution = self._compute_distribution(labeled)
        self.db.commit()
        
        return LabelResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, labeled_count=len(labeled))
    
    # ============ 5. 质量评分 ============
    async def score_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, dimensions: List[str]) -> ScoreResult:
        """
        多维度评分
        """
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status == "processed"
        ).all()
        
        scores = []
        for asset in assets:
            score = await self.scoring_engine.score(asset, dimensions)
            asset.quality_score = score.quality
            asset.aesthetic_score = score.aesthetic
            asset.custom_score = score.custom
            scores.append(score)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 计算数据集平均分
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        dataset.quality_score = sum(s.quality for s in scores) / len(scores) if scores else 0
        self.db.commit()
        
        return ScoreResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, scores=scores, avg_quality=dataset.quality_score)
    
    # ============ 6. 导出数据集 (18种格式) ============
    async def export_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, format: str, 
                             config: Dict = None) -> ExportResult:
        """
        导出数据集 — 18种训练格式
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        dataset.status = "exporting"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 获取资产
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status.in_(["processed", "labeled"])
        ).all()
        
        # 根据格式导出
        if format == "coco":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_coco(assets, config)
        elif format == "yolo":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_yolo(assets, config)
        elif format == "llava":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_llava(assets, config)
        elif format == "webdataset":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_webdataset(assets, config)
        elif format == "jsonl":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_jsonl(assets, config)
        elif format == "parquet":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_parquet(assets, config)
        elif format == "chatsml":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_chatml(assets, config)
        elif format == "dpo":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_dpo(assets, config)
        else:
            raise UnsupportedFormatError(format)
        
        dataset.status = "exported"
        dataset.export_config["last_export"] = {
            "format": format,
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "url": export_url
        }
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.exported",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset_id,
            payload={"format": format, "export_url": export_url}
        )
        
        return ExportResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, format=format, export_url=export_url)
    
    # ============ 7. 数据集版本管理 ============
    async def create_version(self, dataset_id: str, version: str = None, 
                             message: str = None) -> DatasetVersion:
        """
        创建数据集版本
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        new_version = version or increment_version(dataset.version)
        
        # 复制数据集
        versioned = Dataset(
            id=f"ds_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=f"{dataset.name}_v{new_version}",
            modality=dataset.modality,
            version=new_version,
            parent_version_id=dataset.id,
            branch=dataset.branch,
            total_samples=dataset.total_samples,
            total_size_bytes=dataset.total_size_bytes,
            files_count=dataset.files_count,
            label_distribution=dataset.label_distribution,
            quality_score=dataset.quality_score,
            status="ready",
            project_id=dataset.project_id,
            created_by=dataset.created_by,
            owner=dataset.owner,
            storage_backend=dataset.storage_backend,
            storage_bucket=dataset.storage_bucket,
            storage_prefix=dataset.storage_prefix,
            export_config=dataset.export_config,
            source_chain=dataset.source_chain + [{"version": dataset.version, "at": datetime.now().isoformat()}],
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(versioned)
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.versioned",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=versioned.id,
            payload={"version": new_version, "parent": dataset.id}
        )
        
        return versioned
    
    # ============ 8. 数据集统计 ============
    async def get_stats(self, dataset_id: str) -> DatasetStats:
        """
        获取数据集统计信息
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id).all()
        
        # 计算各类统计
        file_types = {}
        label_counts = {}
        quality_distribution = {"high": 0, "medium": 0, "low": 0}
        
        for asset in assets:
            file_types[asset.file_type] = file_types.get(asset.file_type, 0) + 1
            
            if asset.labels:
                for label in asset.labels:
                    label_counts[label.get("name")] = label_counts.get(label.get("name"), 0) + 1
            
            if asset.quality_score:
                if asset.quality_score >= 0.8:
                    quality_distribution["high"] += 1
                elif asset.quality_score >= 0.5:
                    quality_distribution["medium"] += 1
                else:
                    quality_distribution["low"] += 1
        
        return DatasetStats(
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            name=dataset.name,
            modality=dataset.modality,
            total_samples=len(assets),
            file_types=file_types,
            label_distribution=label_counts,
            quality_distribution=quality_distribution,
            avg_quality_score=dataset.quality_score,
            versions=self._get_versions(dataset_id),
            created_at=dataset.created_at
        )
```

### 15.2.1 CapabilityRegistry — 新增双通道执行逻辑

```python
# capabilities_v2/engine.py
class CapabilityRegistry:
    """能力注册中心 — 支持217个能力，区分采集/合成双通道"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._capabilities = {}  # cap_id -> CapabilityDefinition
        self._load_all_definitions()  # 加载217个能力定义
    
    async def invoke(self, cap_id: str, inputs: Dict, actor: str = None, 
                     refs: Dict = None) -> CapabilityResult:
        cap = self._capabilities.get(cap_id)
        if not cap:
            raise CapabilityNotFoundError(cap_id)
        
        # 根据能力类型路由到对应执行器 (分层执行)
        if cap.category == "collect":
            # 采集层 — 只执行真实数据采集，绝不合成
            result = await self._execute_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "synth":
            # 合成层 — 只执行AI模型合成生成
            result = await self._execute_synth(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "clean":
            result = await self._execute_clean(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "dedupe":
            result = await self._execute_dedupe(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "label":
            result = await self._execute_label(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "qc":
            result = await self._execute_qc(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "export":
            result = await self._execute_export(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "version":
            result = await self._execute_version(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "lineage":
            result = await self._execute_lineage(cap, inputs, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownCategoryError(cap.category)
        
        # 审计、血缘、指标记录
        await self._post_process(cap, inputs, result, actor)
        
        return CapabilityResult(status="success", outputs=result, 
                                category=cap.category, layer=cap.layer)
    
    async def _execute_collect(self, cap: CapabilityDefinition, inputs: Dict, 
                               refs: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        采集层执行器 — 仅执行真实数据采集，绝不合成
        
        采集方式:
        - crawl: Web爬虫采集
        - import: 公开数据集导入
        - upload: 用户上传
        
        采集渠道: 83个
        """
        path = cap.path  # crawl / import / upload
        
        if path == "crawl":
            return await self._execute_crawler_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif path == "import":
            return await self._execute_import_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif path == "upload":
            return await self._execute_upload_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownCollectPathError(path)
    
    async def _execute_synth(self, cap: CapabilityDefinition, inputs: Dict, 
                             refs: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        合成层执行器 — 仅执行AI模型/规则合成生成
        
        合成方法: 
        - 扩散模型 (文生图/图生图/图像编辑)
        - 视频生成模型 (文生视频/图生视频/多图生视频)
        - 3D生成模型 (文生3D/图生3D/多图生3D)
        - TTS/ASR模型
        - 语言模型 (文本/Agent/多模态)
        """
        model_type = cap.model_type
        phase = cap.phase
        
        # 根据模型类型路由
        if model_type == "text_to_image":
            return await self._synth_t2i(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_image":
            return await self._synth_i2i(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_edit":
            return await self._synth_edit(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text_to_video":
            return await self._synth_t2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_video":
            return await self._synth_i2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "multi_image_to_video":
            return await self._synth_multi_i2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text_to_3d":
            return await self._synth_t2d(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_3d":
            return await self._synth_i2d(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "audio":
            return await self._synth_audio(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text":
            return await self._synth_text(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "agent":
            return await self._synth_agent(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "multimodal":
            return await self._synth_mm(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownModelTypeError(model_type)
    
    async def _synth_t2i(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """文生图合成"""
        # 调用图像生成Provider (Agnes/ComfyUI/SDXL/Flux)
        provider = self._select_provider("image_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_image(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            size=inputs.get("size", "1024x1024"),
            style=inputs.get("style"),
            negative_prompt=inputs.get("negative_prompt"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed"),
            steps=inputs.get("steps", 30)
        )
        return {"images": result.images, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    async def _synth_t2v(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """文生视频合成"""
        provider = self._select_provider("video_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_video(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            duration=inputs.get("duration", 5),
            resolution=inputs.get("resolution", "1080p"),
            fps=inputs.get("fps", 24),
            style=inputs.get("style"),
            negative_prompt=inputs.get("negative_prompt"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed")
        )
        return {"video": result.video, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    async def _synth_t2d(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """文生3D合成"""
        provider = self._select_provider("3d_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_3d(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            format=inputs.get("format", "glb"),
            resolution=inputs.get("resolution", "medium"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed")
        )
        return {"model": result.model, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    # ... 其他合成方法 (i2i, edit, i2v, multi_i2v, i2d, multi_i2d, audio, text, agent, mm)
```

### 15.2.2 新增: DataProductionPipelineEngine (数据生产全链路编排引擎)

```python
# engines/data_production_pipeline_engine.py
class DataProductionPipelineEngine:
    """
    数据生产全链路编排引擎 — 串联采集→清洗→去重→合成→标注→质检→导出
    支持双通道 (采集通道 + 合成通道) 并行生产
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.capability_registry = CapabilityRegistry()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.active_pipelines = {}
    
    async def create_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> str:
        """创建数据生产管线"""
        pipeline_id = f"pipe_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # 根据配置选择通道
        if config.channel == "collection":
            # 采集通道: 采集 → 清洗 → 去重 → 标注 → 质检 → 导出
            stages = self._build_collection_pipeline(config)
        elif config.channel == "synthesis":
            # 合成通道: 合成 → 清洗 → 标注 → 质检 → 导出
            stages = self._build_synthesis_pipeline(config)
        else:
            # 双通道: (采集 + 合成) → 清洗 → 去重 → 标注 → 质检 → 导出
            stages = self._build_dual_pipeline(config)
        
        self.active_pipelines[pipeline_id] = {
            "id": pipeline_id,
            "config": config,
            "stages": stages,
            "status": "created"
        }
        
        return pipeline_id
    
    def _build_collection_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """构建采集通道管线"""
        return [
            Stage("collect", self._get_collect_capability(config)),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("dedupe", self._get_dedupe_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
    
    def _build_synthesis_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """构建合成通道管线"""
        return [
            Stage("synth", self._get_synth_capability(config)),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
    
    def _build_dual_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """构建双通道管线 (采集 + 合成 并行)"""
        return [
            Stage("collect", self._get_collect_capability(config), parallel=True),
            Stage("synth", self._get_synth_capability(config), parallel=True),
            Stage("merge", self._merge_capabilities, depends_on=["collect", "synth"]),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("dedupe", self._get_dedupe_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
```


### 15.3 CrawlerEngine — 智能采集引擎 (完整实现)

```python
# engines/crawler_engine.py
class CrawlerEngine:
    """
    智能采集引擎 — 83渠道统一调度
    核心功能: 采集任务管理、渠道调度、进度监控、断点续传
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.channels = self._load_all_channels()
        self.active_jobs = {}
        self.crawler_pool = AsyncPool(max_workers=50)
        self.source_tracer = SourceTracer()
        self.dedupe_engine = DedupeEngine()
        self.cleaning_engine = CleaningEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    def _load_all_channels(self) -> Dict:
        """加载83个渠道"""
        return {
            # Web爬虫 (10)
            "playwright": PlaywrightCrawler,
            "selenium": SeleniumCrawler,
            "scrapy": ScrapyCrawler,
            "beautifulsoup": BeautifulSoupCrawler,
            # ... 其余73个
        }
    
    async def start_crawl(self, config: CrawlerConfig) -> str:
        """
        启动采集任务
        """
        job_id = f"crawl_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # 验证配置
        self._validate_config(config)
        
        # 创建任务记录
        self.active_jobs[job_id] = {
            "config": config,
            "status": "queued",
            "started_at": datetime.now(),
            "progress": 0,
            "total_estimated": self._estimate_total(config),
            "results": [],
            "errors": [],
            "logs": []
        }
        
        # 异步执行
        asyncio.create_task(self._run_crawl(job_id))
        
        # 审计记录
        await audit_chain.append(
            action="crawler.start",
            actor=config.owner,
            payload={"job_id": job_id, "channel_type": config.channel_type, "seed_urls": config.seed_urls}
        )
        
        return job_id
    
    async def _run_crawl(self, job_id: str):
        """
        执行采集任务的核心逻辑
        """
        job = self.active_jobs[job_id]
        config = job["config"]
        
        try:
            job["status"] = "running"
            
            # 获取对应的爬虫
            crawler = self._get_crawler(config.channel_type, config)
            
            # 启动采集流
            async for raw_doc in crawler.crawl(config.seed_urls):
                # 1. 实时更新进度
                job["progress"] += 1
                
                # 2. 6级去重
                unique_doc = await self.dedupe_engine.dedupe(raw_doc)
                if not unique_doc:
                    job["logs"].append({"type": "duplicate", "url": raw_doc.url})
                    continue
                
                # 3. 8模态清洗
                clean_doc = await self.cleaning_engine.clean(unique_doc, config.cleaning_rules)
                if clean_doc.rejected:
                    job["logs"].append({"type": "rejected", "url": raw_doc.url, "reason": clean_doc.reason})
                    continue
                
                # 4. 自动打标 (如果配置)
                if config.label_schema:
                    labels = await self.label_engine.label(clean_doc, config.label_schema)
                    clean_doc.labels = labels
                
                # 5. 评分 (如果配置)
                if config.scoring_dimensions:
                    scores = await self.scoring_engine.score(clean_doc, config.scoring_dimensions)
                    clean_doc.scores = scores
                
                # 6. 深度溯源
                source_chain = await self.source_tracer.trace(clean_doc)
                clean_doc.source_chain = source_chain
                
                # 7. 存储
                stored_doc = await self._store_document(clean_doc, config)
                job["results"].append(stored_doc.id)
                
                # 8. 推送事件
                await self.bus.record(
                    topic="crawler.document_collected",
                    entity_type="asset",
                    entity_id=stored_doc.id,
                    payload={
                        "job_id": job_id,
                        "source": config.channel_type,
                        "url": raw_doc.url,
                        "progress": job["progress"]
                    }
                )
                
                # 9. 速率限制
                await self._rate_limit(config.rate_limit_rps)
                
                # 10. 检查是否达到上限
                if config.max_pages and job["progress"] >= config.max_pages:
                    break
            
            job["status"] = "completed"
            job["completed_at"] = datetime.now()
            
            await self.bus.record(
                topic="crawler.job_completed",
                entity_type="crawler_job",
                entity_id=job_id,
                payload={"total_documents": len(job["results"]), "errors": len(job["errors"])}
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            job["status"] = "failed"
            job["error"] = str(e)
            job["completed_at"] = datetime.now()
            
            await self.bus.record(
                topic="crawler.job_failed",
                entity_type="crawler_job",
                entity_id=job_id,
                payload={"error": str(e)}
            )
    
    def _get_crawler(self, channel_type: str, config: CrawlerConfig) -> BaseCrawler:
        """工厂方法获取对应渠道的爬虫"""
        crawler_class = self.channels.get(channel_type)
        if not crawler_class:
            raise UnsupportedChannelError(channel_type)
        return crawler_class(config)
    
    async def get_job_status(self, job_id: str) -> Dict:
        """获取任务实时状态"""
        job = self.active_jobs.get(job_id)
        if not job:
            return {"status": "not_found"}
        
        return {
            "status": job["status"],
            "progress": job["progress"],
            "total_estimated": job["total_estimated"],
            "started_at": job["started_at"],
            "completed_at": job.get("completed_at"),
            "results_count": len(job["results"]),
            "errors_count": len(job["errors"]),
            "progress_percentage": (job["progress"] / job["total_estimated"] * 100) if job["total_estimated"] else 0
        }
    
    async def pause_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """暂停任务 (支持断点续传)"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        if self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] not in ["running", "queued"]:
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "paused"
        return True
    
    async def resume_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """恢复任务"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        if self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] != "paused":
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "running"
        asyncio.create_task(self._run_crawl(job_id))
        return True
    
    async def stop_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """停止任务"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "stopped"
        return True
    
    async def _store_document(self, doc: ProcessedDocument, config: CrawlerConfig) -> Asset:
        """存储采集到的文档"""
        asset = Asset(
            id=f"asset_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
            name=doc.filename or doc.url.split("/")[-1],
            file_type=doc.file_type,
            file_format=doc.file_format,
            file_size=doc.size,
            file_hash=doc.hash,
            file_path=await self._upload_to_storage(doc, config),
            source="crawled",
            source_url=doc.url,
            source_chain=doc.source_chain,
            labels=doc.labels,
            quality_score=doc.scores.get("quality") if doc.scores else None,
            aesthetic_score=doc.scores.get("aesthetic") if doc.scores else None,
            status="processed",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(asset)
        self.db.commit()
        return asset
```

### 15.4 WorkbenchEngine — 标注工作台引擎 (完整实现)

```python
# engines/workbench_engine.py
class WorkbenchEngine:
    """
    标注工作台引擎 — 支持10种几何标注
    功能: 任务拉取/心跳/提交、标注保存、AI辅助标注、Active Learning
    """
    
    GEOMETRY_TYPES = {
        "rect": {"fields": ["x", "y", "w", "h"], "min": 0},
        "polygon": {"fields": ["points"], "min_points": 3},
        "point": {"fields": ["x", "y"]},
        "keypoint": {"fields": ["x", "y", "v"]},
        "obb": {"fields": ["x", "y", "w", "h", "theta"]},
        "mask": {"fields": ["rle", "bitmap_url"]},
        "3d_cuboid": {"fields": ["center", "size", "rotation"]},
        "lidar_pointcloud": {"fields": ["points", "intensity"]},
        "3d_bbox": {"fields": ["center", "size", "rotation"]},
        "panoptic": {"fields": ["segments", "relations"]}
    }
    
    TASK_STATES = ["pending", "assigned", "in_progress", "submitted", "approved", "rejected", "blocked"]
    REVIEW_STAGES = ["draft", "self_check", "peer_review", "final_review", "done"]
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.tasks = {}
        self.locks = {}
        self.annotations = {}
        self.db = SessionLocal()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def enqueue_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str = None) -> str:
        """将任务加入队列"""
        task_id = f"task_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
        self.tasks[task_id] = {
            "id": task_id,
            "pack_id": pack_id,
            "status": "pending",
            "assigned_to": None,
            "created_at": datetime.now()
        }
        return task_id
    
    async def pull_next_task(self, worker_id: str, geometry_type: str = None) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """
        拉取下一个任务 (5分钟锁)
        """
        # 查找可用任务
        query = self.db.query(Pack).filter(
            Pack.status == "in_annotation",
            Pack.assignee == None
        )
        if geometry_type:
            query = query.filter(Pack.geometry_type == geometry_type)
        
        pack = query.order_by(Pack.priority.desc(), Pack.created_at).first()
        if not pack:
            return None
        
        # 加锁 (5分钟)
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack.id}"
        if lock_key in self.locks:
            return None
        
        self.locks[lock_key] = {
            "worker": worker_id,
            "acquired_at": datetime.now(),
            "expires_at": datetime.now() + timedelta(minutes=5)
        }
        
        # 更新任务状态
        pack.assignee = worker_id
        pack.status = "in_progress"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 获取资产
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(Asset.id.in_(pack.asset_ids)).all()
        
        return {
            "pack_id": pack.id,
            "task_id": pack.id,
            "assets": [self._asset_to_dict(a) for a in assets],
            "geometry_type": pack.geometry_type,
            "label_schema": pack.label_schema,
            "lock_expires_at": self.locks[lock_key]["expires_at"]
        }
    
    async def heartbeat(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """心跳续锁"""
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key not in self.locks:
            return False
        if self.locks[lock_key]["worker"] != worker_id:
            return False
        
        # 续锁5分钟
        self.locks[lock_key]["expires_at"] = datetime.now() + timedelta(minutes=5)
        return True
    
    async def release_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """释放任务"""
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key not in self.locks:
            return False
        if self.locks[lock_key]["worker"] != worker_id:
            return False
        
        del self.locks[lock_key]
        
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if pack:
            pack.assignee = None
            pack.status = "ready"
            self.db.commit()
        
        return True
    
    async def save_annotation(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str, 
                              annotations: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        """
        保存标注 (支持10种几何类型)
        """
        # 验证几何类型
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if not pack:
            return False
        
        geometry_type = pack.geometry_type
        schema = self.GEOMETRY_TYPES.get(geometry_type)
        if not schema:
            raise UnsupportedGeometryError(geometry_type)
        
        # 验证每个标注
        for ann in annotations:
            self._validate_annotation(ann, schema)
        
        # 保存
        annotation_id = f"ann_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
        self.annotations[annotation_id] = {
            "id": annotation_id,
            "pack_id": pack_id,
            "worker_id": worker_id,
            "annotations": annotations,
            "geometry_type": geometry_type,
            "saved_at": datetime.now()
        }
        
        # 更新pack进度
        pack.completed_items = pack.completed_items + 1
        pack.progress = pack.completed_items / pack.total_items if pack.total_items else 0
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="annotation.saved",
            entity_type="pack",
            entity_id=pack_id,
            payload={"worker_id": worker_id, "count": len(annotations)}
        )
        
        return True
    
    async def submit_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """提交任务"""
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if not pack:
            return False
        
        # 检查是否所有项目已标注
        if pack.completed_items < pack.total_items:
            return False
        
        pack.status = "annotated"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 释放锁
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key in self.locks:
            del self.locks[lock_key]
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="annotation.submitted",
            entity_type="pack",
            entity_id=pack_id,
            payload={"worker_id": worker_id}
        )
        
        return True
    
    def _validate_annotation(self, ann: Dict, schema: Dict):
        """验证单个标注的几何合法性"""
        if "type" not in ann:
            raise ValidationError("Missing type field")
        
        if ann["type"] not in self.GEOMETRY_TYPES:
            raise ValidationError(f"Unsupported geometry type: {ann['type']}")
        
        schema = self.GEOMETRY_TYPES[ann["type"]]
        for field in schema["fields"]:
            if field not in ann:
                raise ValidationError(f"Missing field: {field}")
        
        # 多边形特殊验证
        if ann["type"] == "polygon":
            if len(ann.get("points", [])) < 3:
                raise ValidationError("Polygon must have at least 3 points")
        
        # 矩形验证
        if ann["type"] == "rect":
            if ann.get("w", 0) <= 0 or ann.get("h", 0) <= 0:
                raise ValidationError("Rect must have positive width and height")
    
    def _asset_to_dict(self, asset: Asset) -> Dict:
        return {
            "id": asset.id,
            "name": asset.name,
            "file_type": asset.file_type,
            "file_format": asset.file_format,
            "file_path": asset.file_path,
            "width": asset.width,
            "height": asset.height,
            "metadata": asset.metadata
        }
```

### 16.2 Provider路由与Gateway

```python
# providers/gateway.py
class AIGateway:
    """
    AI Gateway — 统一Provider管理、路由、Fallback、缓存、成本控制
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.registry = ProviderRegistry()
        self.cache = TTLCache(max_size=10000, default_ttl=3600)
        self.circuit_breakers = {}
        self.cost_guard = CostGuard()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    async def invoke(self, provider: str, model: str, prompt: str,
                     prefer: str = "balanced",
                     max_cost_cents: float = None,
                     stream: bool = False,
                     **kwargs) -> InvokeResult:
        """
        统一的AI调用接口
        """
        # 1. 成本检查
        if max_cost_cents:
            estimated_cost = self._estimate_cost(provider, model, prompt)
            if estimated_cost > max_cost_cents:
                raise CostExceededError(f"Estimated cost {estimated_cost}c exceeds limit {max_cost_cents}c")
        
        # 2. 缓存检查 (非流式)
        if not stream:
            cache_key = self._cache_key(provider, model, prompt, kwargs)
            cached = self.cache.get(cache_key)
            if cached:
                return cached
        
        # 3. 熔断器检查
        circuit_key = f"{provider}:{model}"
        if circuit_key in self.circuit_breakers:
            if self.circuit_breakers[circuit_key].is_open():
                # Fallback
                return await self._fallback(provider, model, prompt, **kwargs)
        
        # 4. 获取Provider
        provider_instance = self.registry.get(provider)
        if not provider_instance:
            raise ProviderNotFoundError(provider)
        
        # 5. 调用
        start = time.time()
        try:
            if stream:
                result = await provider_instance.stream(model, prompt, **kwargs)
            else:
                result = await provider_instance.generate(model, prompt, **kwargs)
            status = "success"
            duration = time.time() - start
            
            # 缓存结果
            if not stream:
                self.cache.set(cache_key, result)
            
            # 记录指标
            self.metrics.record_llm_call(provider, model, duration, status)
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            status = "failure"
            # 记录失败
            if circuit_key in self.circuit_breakers:
                self.circuit_breakers[circuit_key].record_failure()
            
            # 尝试Fallback
            return await self._fallback(provider, model, prompt, **kwargs)
    
    async def _fallback(self, primary_provider: str, model: str, prompt: str,
                        **kwargs) -> InvokeResult:
        """Fallback到备用Provider"""
        fallback_providers = self._get_fallback_chain(primary_provider)
        for provider in fallback_providers:
            try:
                provider_instance = self.registry.get(provider)
                result = await provider_instance.generate(model, prompt, **kwargs)
                result._fallback = True
                result._primary_provider = primary_provider
                return result
            except Exception:
                continue
        raise AllProvidersFailedError(f"All fallback providers failed for {primary_provider}")
    
    def _get_fallback_chain(self, provider: str) -> List[str]:
        """获取Fallback链"""
        chains = {
            "openai": ["claude", "deepseek", "qwen"],
            "claude": ["openai", "deepseek", "gemini"],
            "deepseek": ["qwen", "openai", "claude"],
            "agnes": ["deepseek", "qwen", "openai"],
        }
        return chains.get(provider, ["deepseek", "qwen", "openai"])
    
    def route(self, family: str, prefer: str = "cost") -> str:
        """根据偏好路由到最佳Provider"""
        candidates = self.registry.list_by_family(family)
        if not candidates:
            return "mock"
        
        if prefer == "speed":
            return min(candidates, key=lambda p: p.latency_p50).id
        elif prefer == "trust":
            return max(candidates, key=lambda p: p.trust_level).id
        elif prefer == "cost":
            return min(candidates, key=lambda p: p.price_per_1k_input + p.price_per_1k_output).id
        elif prefer == "free":
            free_candidates = [p for p in candidates if p.price_per_1k_input == 0]
            return free_candidates[0].id if free_candidates else candidates[0].id
        
        return candidates[0].id
```

### 16.3 Agnes AI Provider (免费全模态)

```python
# providers/agnes.py
class AgnesProvider:
    """
    Agnes AI Provider — 免费全模态API
    支持: 文本、图像、视频、短剧
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.base_url = "https://platform.agnes-ai.com/api/v1"
        self.api_key = os.getenv("AGNES_API_KEY")
        self.models = {
            "text": "agnes-2.0-flash",
            "image": "agnes-image-2.1-flash",
            "video": "agnes-video-2.0",
            "drama": "agnes-drama-1.0"
        }
    
    async def generate_image(self, prompt: str, size: str = "1024x1024", 
                             quality: str = "standard") -> ImageResult:
        """生成图像 (免费4K)"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/images/generations"
        payload = {
            "model": self.models["image"],
            "prompt": prompt,
            "size": size,  # 1024x1024, 4096x4096
            "quality": quality,
            "n": 1
        }
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.post(url, json=payload, 
                                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return ImageResult(
                    url=data["data"][0]["url"],
                    prompt=prompt,
                    size=size
                )
    
    async def generate_video(self, prompt: str, duration: int = 5,
                             reference_images: List[str] = None) -> VideoResult:
        """生成视频 (免费)"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/videos/generations"
        payload = {
            "model": self.models["video"],
            "prompt": prompt,
            "duration": duration,
            "reference_images": reference_images or []
        }
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.post(url, json=payload,
                                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return VideoResult(
                    url=data["url"],
                    duration=duration,
                    prompt=prompt
                )
```


## 第17章 API设计 (550+端点)

### 17.1 API设计原则

| 原则 | 实现 |
|---|---|
| RESTful | `/api/v1/{resource}` 标准路径 |
| JSON-Schema校验 | Pydantic BaseModel 集中200+个 |
| 错误统一 | HTTPException + 4xx/5xx + 错误码 |
| 限流 | RateLimiter (60/min) + Provider quota |
| 审计 | 所有写操作经audit chain |
| CSRF | 双提交token (cookie + header) |
| CORS | 前端域名白名单 |
| 幂等 | AgentTask.idempotency_key |
| 异步 | 长任务 → AgentTask + 轮询 |
| 分页 | page/page_size + total |
| 版本 | /api/v1/ 前缀，支持向后兼容 |

### 18.4 跨模态RAG (1024-d统一向量空间)

```python
# multimodal/rag.py
class MultimodalRAG:
    """
    跨模态RAG — 1024-d统一向量空间
    支持: 图文/视频文/音文跨模态检索
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vector_store = VectorStore(dim=1024)
        self.encoders = {
            "text": TextEncoder(),
            "image": CLIPEncoder(),
            "audio": AudioEncoder(),
            "video": VideoEncoder()
        }
        self.bm25 = BM25Index()
    
    async def index(self, refs: List[MediaRef]) -> List[str]:
        """索引多模态数据"""
        ids = []
        for ref in refs:
            # 提取特征
            embedding = await self.encoders[ref.modality].encode(ref.content)
            # 存储
            doc_id = await self.vector_store.add(embedding, ref.metadata)
            # 文本索引 (BM25)
            if ref.text:
                self.bm25.add(doc_id, ref.text)
            ids.append(doc_id)
        return ids
    
    async def search(self, query: MediaRef, top_k: int = 5, 
                     hybrid: bool = True) -> List[RetrievedItem]:
        """跨模态检索 (混合检索)"""
        # 向量检索
        query_embedding = await self.encoders[query.modality].encode(query.content)
        vec_results = await self.vector_store.search(query_embedding, top_k)
        
        if not hybrid:
            return vec_results
        
        # BM25检索
        if query.text:
            bm25_results = self.bm25.search(query.text, top_k)
            # 融合 (RRF)
            results = self._reciprocal_rank_fusion(vec_results, bm25_results)
            return results
        
        return vec_results
    
    async def answer(self, query: MediaRef, top_k: int = 5, 
                     llm_call=None) -> Dict:
        """RAG回答"""
        # 1. 检索相关文档
        results = await self.search(query, top_k)
        
        # 2. 构建上下文
        context = "\n".join([r.content for r in results])
        
        # 3. LLM生成答案
        if llm_call:
            answer = await llm_call(context, query.text)
            return {
                "answer": answer,
                "sources": results,
                "context": context
            }
        
        return {"sources": results}
```

```python
# intelligence/crawler/config.py
@dataclass
class CrawlerConfig:
    """爬虫配置 — 操作员可全维度配置"""
    name: str
    channel_type: ChannelType
    seed_urls: List[str]
    
    # 合规
    compliance: str = "strict"  # strict/internal/audit/research
    respect_robots_txt: bool = True
    respect_rate_limit: bool = True
    rate_limit_rps: float = 1.0
    
    # 反爬
    user_agent_pool: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: DEFAULT_UA_POOL)
    proxy_pool: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    rotate_proxy_every: int = 10
    use_browser_fingerprint: bool = True
    captcha_solver: Optional[str] = None
    
    # 选择器
    selectors: Dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)
    wait_selectors: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    click_selectors: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    
    # 深度
    max_depth: int = 0
    max_pages: int = 100
    same_domain_only: bool = True
    
    # 过滤
    url_include_patterns: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    url_exclude_patterns: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    min_content_length: int = 100
    language_filter: Optional[List[str]] = None
    
    # 清洗规则
    cleaning_rules: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    label_schema: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    scoring_dimensions: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: ["quality", "aesthetic"])
    
    # 输出
    output_format: str = "raw"  # raw/markdown/structured/embedding
    extract_metadata: bool = True
    extract_links: bool = True
    extract_images: bool = True
    
    # 存储
    storage_backend: str = "minio"
    storage_bucket: str = "imdf-crawled"
    storage_prefix: str = ""
    
    # 调度
    parallel_workers: int = 4
    rate_per_worker: float = 0.5
    batch_size: int = 100
    
    # 关联
    project_id: Optional[str] = None
    dataset_id: Optional[str] = None
    owner: Optional[str] = None
```

### 19.3 BaseCrawler抽象基类

```python
# intelligence/crawler/base.py
class BaseCrawler(ABC):
    """所有爬虫的基类"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: CrawlerConfig):
        self.config = config
        self.metrics = CrawlerMetrics()
        self.audit_chain = AuditChain()
        self.compliance = ComplianceChecker(config.compliance)
        self.proxy_pool = ProxyPool(config.proxy_pool)
        self.ua_pool = UserAgentPool(config.user_agent_pool)
        self.session = None
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def fetch(self, url: str) -> RawDocument:
        """子类实现具体抓取"""
        pass
    
    async def crawl(self, urls: List[str]) -> AsyncIterator[RawDocument]:
        """标准crawl流程"""
        semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(self.config.parallel_workers)
        
        async def _process(url: str) -> Optional[RawDocument]:
            async with semaphore:
                # 合规检查
                if not await self.compliance.can_fetch(url):
                    self.metrics.blocked += 1
                    return None
                # 限速
                await self._rate_limit()
                # 抓取
                try:
                    doc = await self.fetch(url)
                    self.metrics.fetched += 1
                    return doc
                except Exception as e:
                    self.metrics.errors += 1
                    await self.audit_chain.append(
                        action="crawler.fetch_failed",
                        actor="system",
                        payload={"url": url, "error": str(e)}
                    )
                    return None
        
        tasks = [_process(url) for url in urls]
        for coro in asyncio.as_completed(tasks):
            doc = await coro
            if doc:
                yield doc
                self.metrics.success += 1
    
    async def _rate_limit(self):
        if self.config.respect_rate_limit:
            await asyncio.sleep(1.0 / self.config.rate_limit_rps)
```

### 19.4 WebCrawler实现 (Playwright驱动)

```python
# intelligence/crawler/web_crawler.py
class WebCrawler(BaseCrawler):
    """通用Web爬虫 - JavaScript渲染友好"""
    
    async def fetch(self, url: str) -> RawDocument:
        async with async_playwright() as p:
            browser = await p.chromium.launch(
                headless=self.config.headless,
                proxy={"server": self.proxy_pool.get_next()} if self.proxy_pool.has_proxies() else None
            )
            context = await browser.new_context(
                user_agent=self.ua_pool.get_next(),
                viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
                locale="en-US"
            )
            page = await context.new_page()
            await page.goto(url, wait_until="networkidle", timeout=30000)
            
            # 智能等待
            for sel in self.config.wait_selectors:
                try:
                    await page.wait_for_selector(sel, timeout=5000)
                except:
                    pass
            
            # 滚动触发懒加载
            await page.evaluate("window.scrollTo(0, document.body.scrollHeight)")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(2000)
            
            # 点击翻页
            for sel in self.config.click_selectors:
                try:
                    await page.click(sel)
                    await page.wait_for_timeout(1000)
                except:
                    pass
            
            # 提取
            html = await page.content()
            text = await page.evaluate("() => document.body.innerText")
            images = await page.query_selector_all("img")
            image_urls = [await img.get_attribute("src") for img in images]
            links = await page.query_selector_all("a")
            link_urls = [await link.get_attribute("href") for link in links]
            metadata = await page.evaluate("""() => ({
                title: document.title,
                description: document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]')?.content,
                keywords: document.querySelector('meta[name="keywords"]')?.content,
                og_image: document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]')?.content,
                author: document.querySelector('meta[name="author"]')?.content
            })""")
            
            await browser.close()
            
            return RawDocument(
                url=url,
                content=html,
                content_type="html",
                text=text,
                images=image_urls,
                links=link_urls,
                metadata=metadata,
                title=metadata["title"]
            )
```

### 19.5 自适应爬虫生成器

```python
# intelligence/crawler/auto_generator.py
class AutoCrawlerGenerator:
    """
    自适应爬虫生成 — LLM分析页面结构自动生成专用爬虫
    流程: 抓取样本 → LLM分析DOM → 生成选择器 → 验证≥95% → 注册
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
    
    async def generate(self, seed_url: str, target_count: int = 100) -> CrawlerConfig:
        # 1. 抓取样本 (10页)
        samples = await self._fetch_samples(seed_url, n=10)
        
        # 2. LLM分析结构
        prompt = f"""
        Analyze these 10 pages and identify the CSS selectors for:
        1. Main content area
        2. Title
        3. Author
        4. Date
        5. Images
        6. Pagination
        7. Infinite scroll triggers
        8. Lazy loading triggers
        
        Pages:
        {samples}
        
        Return JSON with selectors.
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        structure = json.loads(response)
        
        # 3. 生成配置
        config = CrawlerConfig(
            name=f"auto_gen_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            channel_type=ChannelType.WEB,
            seed_urls=[seed_url],
            selectors=structure.get("selectors", {}),
            wait_selectors=structure.get("wait_selectors", []),
            click_selectors=structure.get("click_selectors", []),
            max_pages=target_count,
            respect_robots_txt=True,
            rate_limit_rps=2.0
        )
        
        # 4. 验证准确率 (≥95%)
        accuracy = await self._validate(config)
        if accuracy < 0.95:
            raise InsufficientAccuracyError(f"Accuracy {accuracy:.2%} < 95%")
        
        # 5. 注册到爬虫库
        await self.crawler_engine.register_channel(config)
        
        return config
    
    async def _validate(self, config: CrawlerConfig) -> float:
        """验证爬虫准确率"""
        crawler = WebCrawler(config)
        test_urls = config.seed_urls[:5]  # 测试5个页面
        
        correct = 0
        total = 0
        
        async for doc in crawler.crawl(test_urls):
            total += 1
            # 检查是否成功提取了关键内容
            if doc.content and len(doc.content) > 100:
                correct += 1
        
        return correct / total if total > 0 else 0
```

```
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  去重层 (Dedupe Layer) — 8个能力 (6级去重)                                      │  │
│  │  Level 1: URL精确匹配 → Level 2: URL规范匹配 → Level 3: 内容SHA256 →            │  │
│  │  Level 4: pHash (图像) → Level 5: SimHash (文本) → Level 6: 语义去重            │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  标注层 (Annotation Layer) — 22个能力                                           │  │
│  │  · 自动标注 (14个): 图像分类/检测/分割/描述/VQA · 视频描述/分类                │  │
│  │                    · 音频ASR/分类 · 文本分类/NER/摘要 · 3D分类/多模态描述       │  │
│  │  · 人工标注 (8个): 创建任务/分配/提交/审核 · 共识标注 · 审核                   │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  质检层 (QC Layer) — 19个能力                                                   │  │
│  │  · 抽样: 全量/比例抽样/AQL抽样/分层抽样                                         │  │
│  │  · 专项质检: 图像清晰度/色彩/构图 · 视频画质/运动 · 3D网格/贴图                │  │
│  │  · 音频SNR · 文本语法/语义 · 标注准确率/完整性/一致性                          │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  导出层 (Export Layer) — 20个能力                                               │  │
│  │  · 预训练: WebDataset(.tar), Parquet(.parquet)                                  │  │
│  │  · SFT: ChatML(JSONL), 多模态ChatML(JSONL), COCO, YOLO, LLaVA, InternVL         │  │
│  │  · DPO: JSONL, 多模态DPO(JSONL)                                                │  │
│  │  · RL: 排序JSONL, 多模态排序JSONL                                              │  │
│  │  · LoRA: ChatML, 多模态ChatML                                                   │  │
│  │  · 3D: GLB/glTF/OBJ · 音频: WAV/MP3                                            │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  版本管理 + 血缘管理 (Version & Lineage) — 11个能力                              │  │
│  │  · 版本: 创建/分支/标签/回滚/差异/统计                                          │  │
│  │  · 血缘: 追踪/查询/影响分析/可视化/导出                                         │  │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                      ↓                                                  │
│  交付: Dataset (版本化 + 可追溯 + 可审计)                                              │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 20.2 6级去重引擎

```python
# intelligence/processing/dedupe.py
class DedupeEngine:
    """
    6级去重引擎
    Level 1: URL精确匹配
    Level 2: URL规范化匹配
    Level 3: 内容SHA256 hash
    Level 4: 感知hash pHash (图像)
    Level 5: SimHash (文本)
    Level 6: Embedding语义聚类
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.url_exact = set()
        self.url_normalized = set()
        self.content_sha = {}
        self.phash_index = {}
        self.simhash_index = {}
        self.embedding_index = None
        self.phash_threshold = 8  # Hamming距离阈值
        self.simhash_threshold = 4
    
    async def dedupe(self, doc: RawDocument) -> Optional[Document]:
        """多级去重"""
        # Level 1: URL精确匹配
        if doc.url in self.url_exact:
            return None
        self.url_exact.add(doc.url)
        
        # Level 2: URL规范化
        norm_url = self._normalize_url(doc.url)
        if norm_url in self.url_normalized:
            return None
        self.url_normalized.add(norm_url)
        
        # Level 3: 内容SHA256
        content_hash = hashlib.sha256(doc.content.encode()).hexdigest()
        if content_hash in self.content_sha:
            return None
        self.content_sha[content_hash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 4: pHash (图像)
        if doc.content_type == "image":
            phash = await self._compute_phash(doc.content)
            if phash:
                for existing_hash in self.phash_index:
                    if self._hamming_distance(phash, existing_hash) < self.phash_threshold:
                        return None
                self.phash_index[phash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 5: SimHash (文本)
        if doc.content_type == "text":
            simhash = self._compute_simhash(doc.content)
            if simhash:
                for existing_hash in self.simhash_index:
                    if self._hamming_distance(simhash, existing_hash) < self.simhash_threshold:
                        return None
                self.simhash_index[simhash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 6: Embedding聚类 (语义去重)
        # 使用向量相似度 > 0.95 判定为重复
        # 此处省略具体实现
        
        return Document(url=doc.url, content=doc.content, content_type=doc.content_type)
```

### 20.3 8模态清洗引擎

```python
# intelligence/processing/cleaning.py
class CleaningEngine:
    """
    8模态清洗引擎
    支持: 文本/图像/视频/音频/3D/点云/医疗影像/全景
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.watermark_detector = WatermarkDetector()
        self.nsfw_detector = NSFWDetector()
        self.blur_detector = BlurDetector()
        self.html_cleaner = HTMLCleaner()
    
    async def clean(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """根据模态执行清洗"""
        cleaners = {
            "text": self._clean_text,
            "image": self._clean_image,
            "video": self._clean_video,
            "audio": self._clean_audio,
            "3d": self._clean_3d,
            "pointcloud": self._clean_pointcloud,
            "dicom": self._clean_dicom,
            "panoptic": self._clean_panoptic
        }
        
        cleaner = cleaners.get(doc.content_type)
        if not cleaner:
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Unsupported type")
        
        return await cleaner(doc, rules)
    
    async def _clean_text(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """文本清洗"""
        text = doc.content
        
        # HTML去除
        if rules.get("strip_html", True):
            text = BeautifulSoup(text, "html.parser").get_text()
        
        # 编码修复
        text = text.encode("utf-8", errors="ignore").decode("utf-8")
        
        # 语言检测
        lang = detect(text)
        if rules.get("language_filter") and lang not in rules["language_filter"]:
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Language {lang} not allowed")
        
        # 长度过滤
        if len(text) < rules.get("min_length", 100):
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Too short")
        
        # 敏感词过滤
        if rules.get("sensitive_words"):
            for word in rules["sensitive_words"]:
                if word in text:
                    return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Sensitive word: {word}")
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, content=text, metadata={"language": lang, "length": len(text)})
    
    async def _clean_image(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """图像清洗"""
        from PIL import Image
        img = Image.open(doc.path)
        
        # 尺寸过滤
        min_size = rules.get("min_size")
        if min_size:
            if img.width < min_size[0] or img.height < min_size[1]:
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Size {img.width}x{img.height} < {min_size}")
        
        # 水印检测
        if rules.get("no_watermark", True):
            if await self.watermark_detector.detect(img):
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Watermark detected")
        
        # NSFW检测
        if rules.get("no_nsfw", True):
            if await self.nsfw_detector.detect(img):
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="NSFW")
        
        # 模糊检测
        min_sharpness = rules.get("min_sharpness")
        if min_sharpness:
            sharpness = self._calc_sharpness(img)
            if sharpness < min_sharpness:
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Blurry ({sharpness:.2f})")
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, content=img, 
                          metadata={"width": img.width, "height": img.height, "mode": img.mode})
    
    async def _clean_video(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """视频清洗"""
        import cv2
        cap = cv2.VideoCapture(doc.path)
        
        # 黑边检测
        if rules.get("no_black_bars", True):
            has_bars = await self._detect_black_bars(cap)
            if has_bars:
                cap.release()
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Black bars detected")
        
        # 关键帧提取
        if rules.get("extract_keyframes"):
            frames = await self._extract_keyframes(cap, rules.get("keyframe_count", 10))
        else:
            frames = []
        
        # 字幕提取
        if rules.get("extract_subtitles"):
            subtitles = await self._extract_subtitles(doc.path)
        else:
            subtitles = []
        
        cap.release()
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, 
                          metadata={"frames": frames, "subtitles": subtitles})
```


## 第21章 深度溯源系统

```python
# intelligence/crawler/source_tracer.py
class SourceTracer:
    """
    深度溯源系统
    能力: 沿血缘回溯 · WHOS记录 · 许可证追踪 · C2PA验证 · 数字签名
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.c2pa_verifier = C2PAVerifier()
    
    async def trace(self, doc: Document) -> SourceChain:
        """追溯数据来源"""
        chain = SourceChain()
        
        # 1. 直系来源
        if doc.source_url:
            origin = await self._fetch_origin_page(doc.source_url)
            chain.add(origin)
        
        # 2. 沿血缘反查
        lineage = await self.bus.lineage_for("document", doc.id)
        chain.add_ancestors(lineage)
        
        # 3. 许可证验证
        license_info = await self._resolve_license(doc)
        chain.license = license_info
        
        # 4. C2PA验证 (内容真实性)
        c2pa_result = await self.c2pa_verifier.verify(doc.path)
        chain.c2pa = c2pa_result
        
        # 5. 创作者信息 (WHOS)
        whos_info = await self._get_whos_info(doc)
        chain.whos = whos_info
        
        return chain
    
    async def _fetch_origin_page(self, url: str) -> OriginInfo:
        """获取原始来源页面"""
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, timeout=10) as resp:
                html = await resp.text()
                soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
                return OriginInfo(
                    url=url,
                    title=soup.title.string if soup.title else None,
                    description=soup.find("meta", {"name": "description"}).get("content") if soup.find("meta", {"name": "description"}) else None,
                    author=soup.find("meta", {"name": "author"}).get("content") if soup.find("meta", {"name": "author"}) else None,
                    published_at=self._extract_date(soup)
                )
```


## 第22章 自适应爬虫生成器 (完整实现)

```python
# intelligence/crawler/auto_generator.py (完整)
class AutoCrawlerGenerator:
    """
    自适应爬虫生成器 — LLM驱动
    流程: 抓取样本 → LLM分析DOM → 生成选择器 → 验证≥95% → 注册
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
        self.selector_validator = SelectorValidator()
    
    async def generate(self, seed_url: str, target_count: int = 100) -> CrawlerConfig:
        # 1. 抓取样本
        samples = await self._fetch_samples(seed_url, n=10)
        
        # 2. LLM分析DOM结构
        structure = await self._analyze_structure(samples)
        
        # 3. 生成选择器
        selectors = await self._generate_selectors(structure)
        
        # 4. 构建配置
        config = CrawlerConfig(
            name=f"auto_gen_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            channel_type=ChannelType.WEB,
            seed_urls=[seed_url],
            selectors=selectors,
            max_pages=target_count,
            respect_robots_txt=True,
            rate_limit_rps=2.0
        )
        
        # 5. 验证
        accuracy = await self._validate(config)
        if accuracy < 0.95:
            raise InsufficientAccuracyError(accuracy)
        
        # 6. 注册
        await self.crawler_engine.register_channel(config)
        
        return config
    
    async def _analyze_structure(self, samples: List[str]) -> Dict:
        """LLM分析页面结构"""
        prompt = f"""
        Analyze these {len(samples)} HTML samples and identify:
        1. Main content container CSS selector
        2. Title selector
        3. Author selector
        4. Date selector
        5. Image selectors
        6. Pagination selector
        7. Infinite scroll trigger pattern
        8. Lazy loading trigger pattern
        9. Next page link selector
        
        Samples (truncated to first 5000 chars each):
        {[s[:5000] for s in samples]}
        
        Return JSON with selectors.
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        return json.loads(response)
```
